  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5c78daa9-7fe7-43d2-b385-9ee8da2cef15'
      });
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer8788208123946731458">🔥🌟⚡<b>George Hartley wakes up and realizes that he’s lost his memory. He sees a dead woman sitting in a wheelchair. George searches the place and finds himself trapped in a skyscraper. 🏙 Someone left the documents revealing that his ex-colleagues, financial partners, and even intelligence officers had been spying on him, watching his business activity, digging up dirt on him,</b></span>
  <span id="freeText8788208123946731458" style="display:none">🔥🌟⚡<b>George Hartley wakes up and realizes that he’s lost his memory. He sees a dead woman sitting in a wheelchair. George searches the place and finds himself trapped in a skyscraper. 🏙 Someone left the documents revealing that his ex-colleagues, financial partners, and even intelligence officers had been spying on him, watching his business activity, digging up dirt on him, and someone must have poisoned him.</b> ⚡🌟🔥<br /><br />Numerous facts show that George Hartley was <b>one</b> of the <b>most influential investors</b> and <b>traders</b> in <i>London</i> 💰. He was the head of the largest <i>British financial fund</i>.🇬🇧<br /><br />All of a sudden, his enemies make an attempt to kill him, and George Hartley barely <b>escapes</b> the <b>skyscraper</b> 🚁🚖🏎. He shakes off the pursuers, finds a temporary hideout, and continues to collect the information on his life. 👣<br /><br />Soon, George finds out that for many years, he has been engaged in high-level behind-the-scenes machinations as a <b>creator</b> and <b>manipulator</b> of <b>future financial</b> developments, events, international scandals, information wars that affected stock and commodity markets’ prices. For the past several months, he met <i>North Korean leader</i> 🇰🇵and convinced him to launch a missile, 🚀 conducted an operation against <i>Saudi Arabian Oil Company</i> 🇸🇦, and set off a panic in the oil market, held a secret meeting with a <i>Russian oligarch</i> to speculate on sanctions against Russia. 🇷🇺<br /><br />The more facts George Hartley finds out, the more he realizes he misled and <b>deceived thousands</b> of traders and investors, and probably <b>bankrupted</b> them. He hates his past and wants to start a new life. 🏖<br /><br />But his ex-colleagues and enemies don’t let him leave the game. They start using him as a money-making machine, <b>trading</b> and <b>manipulating</b> his <b>life</b> and <b>death</b>. 🔥<br /><br />George Hartley has nothing to do but to declare <b>financial war</b> against them. ⚔ 💥🌏<br /><br />🍀🍀🍀<br /><br />☝<b>
  <u>Dear Reader! Don't forget to <a href="https://amzn.com/B086QBJ4SQ/" rel="nofollow noopener">👉'Look Inside'👈</a> the book and read several chapters! You won't regret it!</u>
</b> 💖💖💖</span>

  <span id="freeText13980526156679002764" style="display:none">The protagonist George Hartley is a man about forty who has lost his memory. And that means that you don't have real friends. When George Hartley finds out that far away, there exist some people who love him, he wants to quit this crazy game. But he can't.<br />Money spoils people. Big money eliminates God, good, human souls...<br /><br />James Hudson showed the world of insane behind-the-scenes speculations of powerful and influential businessmen of the contemporary world. But what is more important, he showed that no money could replace close people.<br />A well-written, solid, splendid novel.</span>

It can be compared to Dan Brown.<br />James Hudson omits needless words. Just a super action-packed plot.<br />And yeah... no need to be a financially savvy person :)<br />Everything is very well explained.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="S. Young" class="user" itemprop="url" name="S. Young" href="/user/show/112971577-s-young">S. Young</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/112971577-s-young?shelf=wall-street-fiction">wall-street-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/112971577-s-young?shelf=financial-thriller">financial-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/112971577-s-young?shelf=espionage-thriller">espionage-thriller</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3272921979" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14288681893425335897">I didn't like the attitudes of George Hartley - the protagonist - toward women.<br/>On the contrary, I admired the character - the owner of the toy shop - a poor man who deserved a much better life.<br/>They are definitely the opposite characters.<br/>I'm not saying that the protagonist is a devil. No! He strives to stop doing bad things. But the big money means <b>moral unfreedom</b> and various ethical dilemmas.<br/><br/>Regarding the financial markets...<br/>It's an unputdownable conspiracy thriller for Wall Street fiction fans.</span>
  <span id="freeText14288681893425335897" style="display:none">I didn't like the attitudes of George Hartley - the protagonist - toward women.<br />On the contrary, I admired the character - the owner of the toy shop - a poor man who deserved a much better life.<br />They are definitely the opposite characters.<br />I'm not saying that the protagonist is a devil. No! He strives to stop doing bad things. But the big money means <b>moral unfreedom</b> and various ethical dilemmas.<br /><br />Regarding the financial markets...<br />It's an unputdownable conspiracy thriller for Wall Street fiction fans.<br />It was interesting for me to learn a lot of things about financial markets.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('eS4q+49ccRYPv/rvi3LDdPwDCnIk7Z1cUHuOAtIF27aXP4K2M3A8AsYJJnSXBUxTNSlCaSjYXINWheGO65CtGg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
